Was he absent-minded when talking on the phone? ? I was speechless. 3ï¸âƒ£After checking in, there was no landline in the room and I could only contact them via WeChat. The room was far from the front desk, and it was difficult to take the luggage on rainy days. I agreed, but no one came after waiting for half an hour. There was a lot of natural noise in the room, including ventilation, air purifier, and creaking noises. It was particularly obvious at night and could not be turned off.

I will never go there again. I suggest that the B&Bs in Chenjiapu Village next door learn how to operate and be worthy of their own pricing instead of just thinking about how to make money from users.
